_defer.push(function() {
	var $sticky = $('.media-box-fixed');
	if ($(document).height() > 7000) {
		var _top = $sticky.offset().top - 45;
		var _offset = $('.foot-links-box').offset();
		var _bottom = _offset ? $(document).height() - _offset.top : 20;
		$sticky.affix({
			offset: {
				top: function (){
					// 由于广告是异步加载的，_top的值在加载完成后可能会变大，这里取到这个最后的值做为affix插件的数据
					// 注意：由于affix插件的特性，在变成affix-bottom之后, $sticky.offset().top会被覆盖，这里的判断条件过滤了这种情况
					_top = $sticky.offset().top - 45 > _top && $sticky.hasClass('affix-top') ?$sticky.offset().top - 45: _top;
					return _top;
				},
				bottom: _bottom
			}
		});
	}
});

	var cproRenderer = function (_ads) {
		var ads = []

		if (_ads) {
			for(var i = 0; i < _ads.length; i++) {
				if (_ads[i].surl.indexOf('58.com') === -1) {
					ads.push(_ads[i])
				}
			}
		}

		var doubleAds = ads.concat(ads) // 双倍展现
		if (doubleAds.length > 6) {
			doubleAds[6] = hardcodeAds[0]
			doubleAds[7] = hardcodeAds[1]
		} else {
			doubleAds = doubleAds.concat(hardcodeAds)
		}

		$list = viewType == 'item' ? $('.list-ad-items').not('.list-no-ads') : $('.table-view').not('.list-no-ads');
		$firstList = $list.first();
		$lastList = $list.last();

		render(doubleAds);
		if($('.youlanMoreBtn')) {
			$('.hide + .table-adsense-item').addClass('hide')
		}
		function isRealPinned($tags) {
			var isReal = false;
			var classes = ['tag-ace','tag-huoji','tag-ding'];
			$tags.each(function(){
				var tagName = $(this).attr('class').split(/\s+/)[1];
				if (classes.indexOf(tagName) != -1) isReal = true;
			});
			return isReal;
		}
		function render(ads) {
			var index = 1;
			if (showTopItems) {
				if (viewType=='item') {
					for (var i = 2; i > 0; i--) {
						$firstList.prepend(renderAd(ads.shift(),'#item_adsense_top_tmpl'));
					}
				} else {
					$list.prepend(renderAd(ads.shift(),'#'+viewType+'_adsense_tmpl'));
				}
			}

			var regularItems = $lastList.find('.item-regular').get();
			var pinnedItems = $lastList.find('.item-pinned:not(.item-youlan)').get();

			var pinnedItemsSize = 0;
			$(pinnedItems).each(function() {
				var $tags = $(this).find('.tag');
				if (isRealPinned($tags)) pinnedItemsSize++;
			});
			var vipItems = pinnedItems.splice(pinnedItemsSize,pinnedItems.length-pinnedItemsSize);
			regularItems = vipItems.concat(regularItems);
			var $regularItems = $(regularItems);

			var i = 0;
			var insertIndex = 0;
			var insertNum = 2;
			for (; i < ads.length; i++) {
				insertIndex += (i % insertNum)^1;
				if (insertIndex > divide) insertNum = 1;
				if (insertIndex <= divide) {
					var insertPlace = insertSize2 * insertIndex;
				} else {
					var insertPlace = insertSize2 * divide + (insertIndex-divide) * insertSize;
				}
				var content = renderAd(ads[i],'#'+viewType+'_adsense_tmpl');
				var insertNode = $regularItems.eq(insertPlace);

				if (!insertNode.length) break;
				insertNode.before(content);
			};
			// 打点一下展现量
			if(Math.random() < 0.01) {
				window.tracker.evt('search_ad_show', {
					num: $('.clearfix.adsense').length,
					ad1: !!$('#s_i_ad1').length,
					ad3: !!$('#s_i_ad3').length,
					ad5: !!$('#s_i_ad5').length,
				})
			}
						function renderAd(ad, templateHolder) {
				if (!ad) return;
				var template = $(templateHolder).html();
				return $.renderAdsense({
					url: ad.curl,
					line1: ad.tit,
					line2: ad.desc,
					visible_url: ad.surl,
					hintword: ad.bid,
					keyword: keyword,
					billing_name: '30024088_11_cpr',
					index: index++,
					imgUrl: ad.imgUrl || '//file.baixing.net/201508/7e396f2e318dcf731b1d62b615e6b76a.png',
				},template);
			}
		}
	}

/* taq 处理 */
$(document).ready(function () {
	var data = [];
	if (_taq.length) {
		data = _taq;
	}
	_taq = {
		push : function(data) {
			switch (data[0]) {
				case 'evt' :
					var attribute = $.extend({
						"_pvid": tracker.lastPvId
						, "_reid": tracker.reid
						, "_city": tracker.city_name
						, "_category": tracker.category
						, "_ad": tracker.adid
						, "_url": document.location.href.length ? document.location.href.substr(0, 4000) : ''
						, "_bnid": Cookie.read('kjj_trace_banner_id')
						, "_clid": Cookie.read('kjj_trace_click_id_new')
						, "_prof": Cookie.read('kjj_trace_profile_new')
						, "_refer": document.referrer.length ? document.referrer : ''
					}, data[2]);
					$.get('/c/ev/' + encodeURIComponent(data[1]), attribute);
					break;
				case 'ic' :
					$.get( '/c/ic/' + encodeURIComponent(data[1]));
					break;
				case 'count' :
					$.get( '/c/mc/' + encodeURIComponent(data[1]) + '.' + encodeURIComponent(data[2]));
					break;
				case 'timing' :
					$.get('/c/tm/' + encodeURIComponent(data[1]) + '.' + encodeURIComponent(data[2]) +
					'.' + encodeURIComponent(data[3]))
					break;
				case 'klog' :
					$.get( '/c/klog/' + encodeURIComponent(data[1]), data[2]);
					break;
				case 'perf' :
					$.get('/c/perf/' + encodeURIComponent(data[1]), data[2]);
					break;
				case 'manageTrack' :
					$.get('/c/mt/' + encodeURIComponent(data[1]), data[2]);
					break;
			}
		}
	};
	while (data.length) {
		_taq.push(data.shift());
	}
});
</script>

(function() {
	function b64EncodeUnicode(str) {
		return btoa(encodeURIComponent(str).replace(/%([0-9A-F]{2})/g, function(match, p1) {
			return String.fromCharCode('0x' + p1);
		}));
	}

	$('.ex_re').on('click', function(e) {
		var $el = $(e.target)
		var link = $el.attr('href')

		if(!$el.data('url')) $el.data('url', link)

		var extra = { url: $el.data('url'), href: window.location.href }
		var encodeLink = b64EncodeUnicode($.param({url: link, eventType: 'external_redirect', eventValue: extra})).toString()
		var redirectUrl = 'http://www.baixing.com/redirect/index?r=' + encodeLink.replace('+', '-').replace('_', '/').replace('=', ',')

		$el.attr('href', redirectUrl)
	})
})();
</script><script type='text/javascript'>
(function() {
	var clickedAdsense = []

	$('body').on('adsense_click', function(event, data) {
		if(!data || !data.id) return false

		var id = '#' + data.id
		if(clickedAdsense.indexOf(id) === -1) {
			clickedAdsense.push(id)
		} else {
			setTimeout(function() {
				$(id).remove()
			}, 1000)
		}
	})

	// 暂时检测一下搜索广告点击状况，就不取全量了
	if (Math.random() < 0.1) {
		$('body').on('click', '.media.clearfix.adsense', function(e) {
			var offset = $(e.target).parents('.adsense').offset()
			var posY = offset.top - $(window).scrollTop()
			var posX = offset.left - $(window).scrollLeft()

			var result = {
				x: e.screenX - posX,
				y: e.screenY - posY - 120
			}

			tracker.evt('search_ad_click_position', result)
		})
	}
})();
